<a id="1919" class="Keyword">private</a> <a id="1927" class="Keyword">variable</a>  <a id="1937" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1937" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="1939" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1939" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a> <a id="1942" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1942" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="1944" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1944" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a> <a id="1947" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1947" class="Generalizable">Î³</a> <a id="1949" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1949" class="Generalizable">Ïá¶œ</a> <a id="1952" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1952" class="Generalizable">Î¹</a> <a id="1954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1956" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a>

Recall, `f ~ g` means f and g are *extensionally* (or pointwise) equal; i.e., `âˆ€ x, f x â‰¡ g x`. We use this notion of equality of functions in the following definition of *isomorphism*.

We could define this using Sigma types, like this.

```agda
_â‰…_ : {Î± Î² : Level}(ğ‘¨ : Algebra Î± ğ‘†)(ğ‘© : Algebra Î² Ïáµ‡) â†’ Type(ğ“ âŠ” ğ“¥ âŠ” Î± âŠ” Î²)
ğ‘¨ â‰… ğ‘© =  Î£[ f âˆˆ (hom ğ‘¨ ğ‘©)] Î£[ g âˆˆ hom ğ‘© ğ‘¨ ] ((âˆ£ f âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ g âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘© âˆ£) Ã— (âˆ£ g âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ f âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘¨ âˆ£))
```

However, with four components, an equivalent record type is easier to work with.

   <a id="3470" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="3479" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3479" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3483" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3485" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2798" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3488" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3490" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3494" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3495" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3497" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2814" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3502" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3504" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3508" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3450" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3509" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3511" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2676" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3514" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3516" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2798" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3519" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3521" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3526" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3528" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2814" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3533" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3535" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3539" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3454" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3540" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="3545" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3479" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3547" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3549" href="Function.Bundles.html#2113" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="3554" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3556" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2798" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3559" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3561" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3457" class="Bound">xy</a>
   <a id="3567" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3567" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3572" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3574" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3450" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3576" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2676" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3579" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3454" class="Bound">y</a>
   <a id="3584" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3567" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3589" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3591" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2706" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3599" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2690" class="Function">symâ‚‚</a> <a id="3604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3605" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2832" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3613" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3450" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3614" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3618" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2706" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3625" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3479" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3628" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2832" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3636" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3454" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3637" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

That is, two structures are *isomorphic* provided there are homomorphisms going back and forth between them which compose to the identity map.


#### <a id="properties-of-isomorphisms-of-setoid-algebras">Properties of isomorphism of setoid algebras</a>

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3921" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3926" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2723" class="Module Operator">_â‰…_</a>

  <a id="5042" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="5050" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5050" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="5055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5057" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5020" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a> <a id="5060" href="Relation.Binary.Bundles.html#1184" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆ</a> <a id="5062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5063" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5006" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5065" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="5069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5070" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4998" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="5072" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1879" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="5076" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5020" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a><a id="5078" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="5154" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5105" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5159" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5161" href="Function.Bundles.html#2113" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="5166" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5006" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5168" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5028" class="Bound">fafb</a>

  <a id="5241" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5224" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="5246" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5248" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1226" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5254" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5050" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="5259" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5260" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1226" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5266" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5105" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5271" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5175" class="Function">lem3</a><a id="5275" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="5279" class="Comment">-- The &quot;from&quot; map of an isomorphism is injective.</a>
<a id="â‰…fromInjective"></a><a id="5329" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5329" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5344" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="5347" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5348" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5348" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5352" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2709" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5360" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1937" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="5362" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1939" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a><a id="5364" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5366" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5366" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a> <a id="5368" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5370" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2709" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5378" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1942" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="5380" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1944" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a><a id="5382" class="Symbol">}</a>
                  <a id="5402" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5403" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5403" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5405" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5407" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5348" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5409" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2723" class="Record Operator">â‰…</a> <a id="5411" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5366" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a><a id="5412" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5414" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5416" href="Setoid.Functions.Injective.html#2150" class="Function">IsInjective</a> <a id="5428" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="5430" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2814" class="Field">from</a> <a id="5435" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5403" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5437" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a>

<a id="5440" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5329" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5455" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5455" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5457" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5459" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4926" class="Function">â‰…toInjective</a> <a id="5472" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5473" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4066" class="Function">â‰…-sym</a> <a id="5479" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5455" class="Bound">Ï†</a><a id="5480" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Fortunately, the lift operation preserves isomorphism (i.e., it's an *algebraic
invariant*). As our focus is universal algebra, this is important and is what
makes the lift operation a workable solution to the technical problems that arise
from the noncumulativity of Agda's universe hierarchy.

<pre class="Agda">

           <a id="6759" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6760" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6368" class="Function">Lift-Alg-isoÊ³</a> <a id="6774" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5851" class="Function">Lift-â‰…Ë¡</a><a id="6781" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

The lift is also associative, up to isomorphism at least.

<a id="7494" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7374" class="Function">Lift-assoc&#39;</a><a id="7505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7506" class="Argument">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="7508" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7510" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7510" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a><a id="7511" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7513" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7513" class="Bound">Î²</a><a id="7514" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7516" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7516" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="7517" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7519" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7521" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4161" class="Function">â‰…-trans</a> <a id="7529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7530" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4066" class="Function">â‰…-sym</a> <a id="7536" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6074" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a><a id="7542" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7544" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7545" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4161" class="Function">â‰…-trans</a> <a id="7553" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6074" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a> <a id="7560" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6074" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a><a id="7566" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Products of isomorphic families of algebras are themselves isomorphic. The proof
looks a bit technical, but it is as straightforward as it ought to be.

<pre class="Agda">

   <a id="8765" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8727" class="Function">Ïˆâˆ¼Ï•</a> <a id="8769" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8769" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8771" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8773" class="Symbol">Î»</a> <a id="8775" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8775" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="8777" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8779" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2886" class="Field">fromâˆ¼to</a> <a id="8787" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8788" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8112" class="Bound">AB</a> <a id="8791" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8775" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8792" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8794" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8769" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8796" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8775" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8797" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

A nearly identical proof goes through for isomorphisms of lifted products.

<pre class="Agda">
